<pr_description>
[sm6.10] coopvec input vec type convert
**Description**
There is a simple convert from f16 to fp8 for input vec, however, the dxil looks incorrect.
hlsl:
typedef vector<half, 16> half16;
half16 srcF16 = inbuf.Load<half16>(0);
InterpretedVector<uint, 4, ComponentEnum::F8_E4M3FN> converted =
      Convert<ComponentEnum::F8_E4M3FN, ComponentEnum::F16>(srcF16);

dxil:
  %4 = call %dx.types.ResRet.v16f16 @dx.op.rawBufferVectorLoad.v16f16(i32 303, %dx.types.Handle %3, i32 0, i32 undef, i32 2)  ; RawBufferVectorLoad(buf,index,elementOffset,alignment)
  %5 = extractvalue %dx.types.ResRet.v16f16 %4, 0
  %6 = shufflevector <16 x half> %5, <16 x half> undef, <4 x i32> <i32 0, i32 1, i32 2, i32 3>
  %7 = call <4 x i32> @dx.op.linAlgConvert.v4i32.v4f16(i32 -2147483618, **<4 x half> %6**, i32 8, i32 21)  ; LinAlgConvert(**inputVector**,inputInterpretation,outputInterpretation)

we expected <16 x half> %5 as the convert input, but it shufflevector to <4xhalf> which is not expected.

Is there something wrong from this hlsl or dxc problem

  3736	      case LICOMPTYPE_VK_BUFFER_POINTER: {
  3737	        const ArBasicKind *match =
  3738	            std::find(g_ArBasicKindsAsTypes,
  3739	                      &g_ArBasicKindsAsTypes[_countof(g_ArBasicKindsAsTypes)],
  3740	                      AR_OBJECT_VK_BUFFER_POINTER);
  3741	        DXASSERT(match !=
  3742	                     &g_ArBasicKindsAsTypes[_countof(g_ArBasicKindsAsTypes)],
  3743	                 "otherwise can't find constant in basic kinds");
  3744	        size_t index = match - g_ArBasicKindsAsTypes;
  3745	        paramTypes.push_back(
  3746	            m_sema->getASTContext().getTypeDeclType(m_objectTypeDecls[index]));
  3747	        break;
  3748	      }
  3749	#endif
  3750	      default:
  3751	        DXASSERT(false, "Argument type of intrinsic function is not "
  3752	                        "supported");
  3753	        break;
  3754	      }
  3755	    }
  3756	    return paramTypes;
  3757	  }
  3758	
  3759	  QualType getIntrinsicFunctionType(
  3760	      const SmallVectorImpl<QualType> &paramTypes,
  3761	      const SmallVectorImpl<ParameterModifier> &paramMods) {
  3762	    DXASSERT(!paramTypes.empty(), "Given param type vector is empty");
  3763	
  3764	    ArrayRef<QualType> params({});
  3765	    if (paramTypes.size() > 1) {
  3766	      params = ArrayRef<QualType>(&paramTypes[1], paramTypes.size() - 1);
  3767	    }
  3768	
  3769	    FunctionProtoType::ExtProtoInfo EmptyEPI;
  3770	    return m_sema->getASTContext().getFunctionType(paramTypes[0], params,
  3771	                                                   EmptyEPI, paramMods);
  3772	  }
  3773	
  3774	  void SetParmDeclsForIntrinsicFunction(
  3775	      TypeSourceInfo *TInfo, FunctionDecl *functionDecl,
  3776	      const SmallVectorImpl<ParmVarDecl *> &paramDecls) {
  3777	    FunctionProtoTypeLoc Proto =
  3778	        TInfo->getTypeLoc().getAs<FunctionProtoTypeLoc>();
  3779	
  3780	    // Attach the parameters
  3781	    for (unsigned P = 0; P < paramDecls.size(); ++P) {
  3782	      paramDecls[P]->setOwningFunction(functionDecl);
  3783	      paramDecls[P]->setScopeInfo(0, P);
  3784	      Proto.setParam(P, paramDecls[P]);
  3785	    }
